* From 26/09/25, students will come to school only on the day of the exam.
Oct 05, 2025 8:26 pm

Parth Sharma

* From 26/09/25, students will come to school only on the day of the exam.
* Drawing/ICT exam will be held on 25/09/25.
* Students of classes 6 to 12 will come to school at 8:30 am.
* Assembly will be held from 8:30 to 8:50 and then they will sit in their rooms as per the seating plan.
* After the exam, mid-day meal will be provided to classes 6 to 8.
* Exam timings for classes 6, 7, and 8 will be from 9:30 am to 12:00 pm.
* Exam timings for classes 9 to 12 will be from 9:30 am to 12:30 pm.
* The class teacher will inform all the students of their class about their Student ID and Roll no. * The class teacher will obtain an undertaking from the parents of all students whose attendance is less than 75%.

* If a student is absent from the mid-term exam due to illness, the parents must submit a medical certificate from a registered medical practitioner within three days.

* The invigilator will check all entries on the first page of the answer sheet and sign it with their Emp ID. They must also sign on the last page where the student completes their answer. Blank pages must be crossed out.

* The online marks entry link will be open from 27/09/25 to 5/11/25.

* Carefully read and meticulously follow the examination circular sent by the Department of Education.

* The class teacher will ask students to note the date sheet.

* Maintain contact with students via WhatsApp and send messages daily regarding which subject's exam is scheduled.

The Principal
